DROP table Line CASCADE;
DROP table Station CASCADE;
DROP table Train CASCADE;
Drop table Service CASCADE;
Drop table Incident CASCADE;
Drop table Car CASCADE;

CREATE TABLE Line  (
                    LineName                 text           NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
                    OpenDate                 date,
                    Terminals                  text,
                    NumberOfStops        smallint,
                    CHECK (NumberOfStops >0),
                    Length                      Float,
                    Power                       text,
                    CHECK (Power IN ('Overhead Line',
                                                 'Third Rail',
                                                 'Supercapacitor')),
                    CarType                    text,
                    CHECK (Cartype IN ('A',
                                                   'B',
                                                   'L',
                                                   'D',
                                                   'APM',
                                                   'Tram')),
                    CarNo                       smallint,
                    CHECK (CarNo > 1),
                    Depots                      text,
                    CtrlCenter                 text,
                    Gauge                       text,
                    CHECK (Gauge IN ('Standard Gauge',
                                                 'Rubber Tyres')),
                    Status                       text NOT NULL);


CREATE TABLE station
(                      StationName          text            NOT NULL,
                       FormerName          text            NULL,
                       OpenDate              date           NOT NULL,
                       LineName               text           NOT NULL REFERENCES Line(LineName) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
                       StationNo               smallint     NOT NULL,
                       FormerLine             text           REFERENCES Line(LineName) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
                       Grade                      text           NOT NULL,
                       NoOfPlatforms        smallint     NOT NULL,
                       PlatformType          text            NOT NULL,
                       City                         text            NOT NULL,
                       District                    text            NOT NULL,
                       PSD                        text             NULL,
                       Transfers                 text             NULL,
                       PRIMARY KEY (StationName, LineName, StationNo),
                       CHECK (Grade IN('Underground',
                                                   'At-grade',
                                                   'Elevated')),
                       CHECK (StationNo >=1),
                       CHECK (NoOfPlatforms >=1),
                       CHECK (City IN('Guangzhou',
                                               'Foshan')),
                       CHECK (District IN('Conghua',
                                                    'Zengcheng',
                                                    'Huadu',
                                                    'Baiyun',
                                                    'Yuexiu',
                                                    'Liwan',
                                                    'Tianhe',
                                                    'Haizhu',
                                                    'Panyu',
                                                    'Nansha',
                                                    'Huangpu',
                                                    'Shunde',
                                                    'Chancheng',
                                                    'Nanhai'))
);










CREATE TABLE Train
(                      CarType                                  text            NOT NULL,
                       CHECK (Cartype IN ('A',
                                                      'B',
                                                      'L',
                                                      'D',
                                                      'APM',
                                                      'Tram')),
                       CarName                                 text               NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
                       NickName                              text                NULL,
                       Model                                    text                NULL,
                       Quantity                               smallint            NULL,
                       CHECK (Quantity >=1),
                       CarNo                                   smallint           NOT NULL,
                       CHECK (CarNo >=1),
                       Manufacturer                          text                NOT NULL,
                       Country                                  text                 NOT NULL,
                       YearOfManufacturing             smallint           NOT NULL,
                       Servein1                                  text                NOT NULL REFERENCES Line (Linename) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
                       Servein2                                  text                REFERENCES Line (linename) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
                        PIS                                         text                NULL,
                       Power                                     text                 NOT NULL,
                       CHECK (Power IN ('Overhead Line',
                                                    'Third Rail',
                                                    'Supercapacitor')),
                       Gauge                                     text                 NOT NULL,
                        CHECK (Gauge IN ('Standard Gauge',
                                                     'Rubber Tyres')),
                       MaxSpeed                               smallint           NOT NULL);

CREATE TABLE Service
(                      ServiceName                           text                  NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
                       LineName                               text                  NOT NULL REFERENCES Line ON DELETE RESTRICT,
                       FirstStop                                 text                  NOT NULL,
                       LastStop                                  text                  NOT NULL,
                       NumberOfStops                    integer                NOT NULL,
                       CHECK (NumberOfStops >1),
                       StopingAt                                 text,
                       Status                                     text                   NOT NULL,
                       FirstTrainHrs                           integer,
                       FirstTrainMin                          integer,
                       LastTrainHrs                           integer,
                       LastTrainMin                           integer,
                       CHECK (FirstTrainHrs <24),
                       CHECK (FirstTrainMin <60),
                       CHECK (LastTrainHrs <24),
                       CHECK (LastTrainMin <60));

CREATE TABLE Incident
(                       IncidentDate                          date                    NOT NULL,
                        Nature                                   text                     not null,
                        Linename                               text                     not null REFERENCES Line(Linename) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
                        Stationname                           text,
                        Description                             text                     not null,
                        Deaths                                    integer                not null,
                        Injuries                                   integer                 not null,
                        CHECK (Deaths >=0),
                        CHECK (Injuries >=0),
                        PRIMARY KEY (IncidentDate, Linename));


CREATE TABLE Car
(                       CarID                                       integer                NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
                        CarNumbering                         text                     NOT NULL,
                        FormerNumbering                    text,
                        CarName                                 text                       NOT NULL REFERENCES Train ON DELETE RESTRICT,
                        LineName                                 text                     NOT NULL REFERENCES Line ON DELETE RESTRICT,
                        FormerLine                              text                       REFERENCES Line ON DELETE RESTRICT,
                        FormationID                            integer                   REFERENCES Car(CarID) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
                        FormerFormation                      text,
                        Note                                         text);
